ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Flying_ship=A Flying Ship can be used to travel between larger islands. <cf>Flying Ships that you can take control of contain a Flying Ship Core. To take control of a Flying Ship, you need to place and interact with its Cockpit. <cf>Once you place the Cockpit, your Home Point is set to that Ship, meaning that upon death, you will respawn there, and using the Starter Compass will teleport you directly to it. <cf>If the Cockpit is destroyed, the Home Point linked to that Flying Ship will be lost.
ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Altitude=Altitude in the game affects the biomes you encounter at different heights. As you ascend, enemies become tougher, and the Loot from Dungeons improves. Higher altitudes also unlock better recipes. To reach these elevated areas, you'll need to upgrade your Flying Ship using a Flying Ship Core and with Enhanced Balloons, allowing you to fly higher and access more challenging and rewarding locations.
ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Armor_crafting=Armor crafting can only be done at the Smithing Station. To craft an Armor piece, you first need to know its recipe. Once you have the recipe, go to the Smithing Station, select the Armor piece you wish to create, and if you have the required materials, press the "Craft" button to create the selected item. <cf><cf>Armor pieces provide Defense, which helps reduce the Damage taken from enemy attacks, and they also have a Durability value.
ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Repair=As items lose Durability, their effectiveness gradually decreases. When items break completely, they lose all functionality. Damaged or broken Tools, Weapons, and Equipment can be repaired using Repair Kits. These kits can be used anywhere, but they restore less Durability compared to using them at an Anvil. Higher-quality Anvils allow for even more efficient repairs, making them a valuable resource for maintaining your Gear.
ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Baloons=Balloons are essential for increasing the Flying Ship's altitude, allowing it to rise to greater heights. To use Balloons, they must be connected to a power source, such as an Energy Generator, via Pipes.<cf><cf>Better-quality Balloons enable the Flying Ship to reach even higher altitudes, improving its overall capabilities, as long as the Flying Ship Core is upgraded to support those altitude levels. Make sure to keep your Flying Ship powered to maintain the Balloons' effectiveness and maximize your flying potential.
ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Balloons_Short=Balloons increase a Flying Ship's altitude and must be powered via Pipes from a Generator.

ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Bow_and_Arrows=Bows are two-handed Weapons that require Arrows to function. The bow determines the base Damage, while the Arrow Type provides additional Effects.<cf><cf>To fire an Arrow, hold {PrimaryAction} to draw the bow—the longer you hold it, the more powerful the shot, increasing both range and Damage. Pressing {SecondaryAction} while drawing cancels the shot.<cf><cf>If you have multiple types of Arrows in your Inventory, you can switch between them while holding a bow in your Hotbar. Hold {ShowRadial} to open the Arrow selection wheel and use the {ItemBarScroll} to cycle through available Arrow Types.

ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Combat_Basic=Combat revolves around the use of Weapons, each with its own Damage value. Every attack consumes Stamina and reduces the Durability of the Weapon. A single {PrimaryAction} press performs a quick attack, while repeatedly pressing executes a fast attack combo. Holding {PrimaryAction} charges a strong attack, and moving in one of the four basic directions while holding {PrimaryAction} triggers a directional strong attack suited to the movement. {SecondaryAction} is used to block incoming attacks. Each attack has a chance to deal Critical Damage, with increased odds when striking an enemy from behind or attacking while hidden.
ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Combat_Basic_Short=Combat uses Weapons that consume Stamina.<cf>Press {PrimaryAction} for quick attacks,<cf>Hold {PrimaryAction} for a strong attack,<cf>Use {SecondaryAction} to block.

Each item can hold only one rune effect. Once the target item is selected, the rune and dust are consumed, and the Equipment becomes infused with the rune's power.<cf><cf>Infused items can also be placed into a Processing Station to extract a rune with a weaker effect than the one originally infused into the item, allowing partial recovery of rune power.

ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Alchemy=To create Potions, you need an Alchemy Station, Magical Liquid, and Alchemy Ingredients. ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Farming_Basic=To grow crops, you need a Pot or Incubator, a seedling, the correct Soil, and a watering item. Start by placing the appropriate Soil in the Pot or Incubator, then insert a seedling that can grow in that specific Soil. You can check which Soil a seedling needs in its item description or in the Compendium. After planting, use the watering item to hydrate the Soil. As long as the crop remains watered, it will continue to grow. If the crop isn't watered, its growth will stop, and it will start to rot. You can stop the rotting by watering it again, which will resume the growth process.<cf><cf>The time it takes for a crop to grow or rot, and the rate at which it consumes Water, depends on the specific plant. Crops also begin to rot if they are placed in the wrong Soil or if a potted plant is placed at an incorrect Altitude. However, crops in an Incubator don't have Altitude restrictions. You can find the required Altitude for a crop in the seedling's description or the Compendium.
ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Generator=To power devices on a Flying Ship, you need Energy, which is produced using Generators. To generate Energy, interact with a Generator, place a suitable Fuel source (wood, coal, etc.) into the Fuel Slot, and press "Start". The inserted Fuel will be consumed, producing Energy for a set duration. However, once the Generator is activated, Energy starts depleting immediately, regardless of whether any devices are connected. To stop Energy consumption, press "Stop" at any time.<cf><cf>Each Generator produces a fixed amount of Energy using Fuel. More advanced Generators can use higher-efficiency Fuels to produce more Energy or for longer periods.

ST_TutorialsDescriptions::Desc_Tut_Basic=You have several key stats, including Health, Stamina, Defense, Oxygen, Experience, and Level. To heal beyond this limit, you must consume Potions or Food. Automatic regeneration activates 5 seconds after taking no further Damage.<cf><cf>Stamina is consumed when performing actions like running, fast swimming, combat, or mining.
